Hangzhou 96

▲ Two Suicides Due to Economic Pressure Jiang Tongsheng, from Keqiao, Shaoxing, used to work as a hotel clerk in Shanghai. Due to the impact of the war, he had been unemployed for a long time. Yesterday, he came to Hangzhou to seek help from his uncle, Jiang Yuanhui, and his aunt, who ran the Xudasheng Rice Store in Baoyufang, to borrow money to find another job. Unexpectedly, he was ridiculed and scolded. Jiang was stimulated by this and went directly to Jianggan to take the Yidu ferry across the river. Fortunately, the old ferryman Zhou Ahong noticed and managed to rescue him and send him to the public security bureau for repatriation to Shanghai. Hua Huanzhang, from Shaoxing, was also suffering from poverty and illness and was unable to maintain himself economically. He also committed suicide by jumping into the river yesterday afternoon. He was rescued by the No. 8 Yidu tugboat and sent to the police station, which transferred him to the provincial relief center for assistance.

▲ Site Selected for Shanghai Arsenal In order to avoid being destroyed by the Japanese, important parts of the Shanghai Arsenal were continuously transported to Zhejiang Province during the Shanghai war. There was a previous proposal to convert the Hangzhou Mint into an arsenal. At that time, Wang Zhuzhai, the chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, sent a letter to Chen Gongxia, the Deputy Minister of Military Affairs, requesting him to withdraw the order. Chen replied and cancelled the proposal. Now, the central authorities of the factory have decided to move to Hangzhou. A few days ago, Hu Sihong, the director of the inspection department of the factory, and Lin Weirong, the director of the ammunition factory, came to Hangzhou to look for a factory site. They have already selected a site near the Zhakou area. In terms of transportation, there are five or six sections of buses that can pass through the area. It is planned to purchase 300 mu of land, with a price of 50 yuan per mu. The construction cost is estimated to be about 500,000 yuan. The project will take about half a year to complete. Director Hu and Director Lin have consulted with Factory Director Song and submitted a request to the Ministry of Military Affairs for approval to proceed.

▲ Military Department Sends Personnel to Escort Robber from Longjing On the 28th of last month, four Cantonese pilgrims, including Tan Diguang, were robbed near Longjing, West Lake, by a person wearing a military uniform, losing 20 yuan in paper money. After reporting to the police, Zheng Zhong, a major officer of the Aviation School, was arrested near the Shiwu Cave and handed over to the Provincial Public Security Bureau Martial Law Command for interrogation. He confessed without hesitation. Later, Mao Bangchu, the principal of the Aviation School, jointly interrogated him and completely overturned his previous confession. Mao has submitted a request to the Ministry of Military Affairs to organize a special court for trial. It is now reported that the Military Department, after receiving the report, has sent personnel with documents to Zhejiang to escort him to Beijing for trial. It is reported that this province has not yet agreed to the request, or the Ministry will send personnel to Zhejiang to conduct a joint trial to ensure thoroughness.

Ningbo 97

▲ Results of the Bandit Suppression Conference The military and political authorities of the three counties of Feng, Xin, and Sheng, and representatives of the agencies, held a bandit suppression conference at the Sheng County Chamber of Commerce on the afternoon of the 6th. The resolutions passed were: (1) In the future, after bandits are captured, a request will be made to the provincial government for permission to execute them on the spot to deter the bandits. (2) Measures for punishing the families of bandits. (3) Assigning county and township chiefs to secretly report the names and residences of bandits. (4) If bandits from this county flee into neighboring counties, the bandit suppression military and police can pursue them into neighboring counties. At the same time, the military and police of neighboring counties must also send teams to assist. (5) Reward measures for military and police who kill bandit leaders.

▲ Children Kidnapped and Redeemed Halfway Xu Shuichao, a resident of Yanglutou, Wanan Township, 5th District of Yuyao, is relatively well-off. On the night of the day before yesterday, more than a dozen bandits suddenly came, holding pistols and flashlights, and broke into his house. At that time, Shuichao heard the sound of the door being broken and knew there was a bandit alarm, so he escaped through the back door. When the bandits entered the house and did not see Shuichao, they kidnapped his twelve-year-old son and ten-year-old daughter. Later, someone came out to plead, and as a result, the hostages were redeemed for 700 yuan halfway.

▲ Heavy Thunderstorm in Ningbo Since the beginning of summer, the weather in Ningbo has not been very hot. The weather suddenly became hot starting on the 5th. Yesterday (the 6th) at around 4:00 PM, there was a sudden thunderstorm. Its momentum was very strong. By about 6:00 PM, the streets were filled with water, and the river suddenly rose, exceeding the river bank by more than a foot. At 10:30 PM, the thunderstorm struck again, and with a clap of thunder, the electricity of the whole city was absorbed, suddenly plunging it into darkness. Everyone was shocked, but the light was restored immediately, and there was no danger.

▲ Thief Escapes Due to Robbery Ling Yixing, a thief from Kentou in Linhaibei Township, was sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment by the local judicial branch. The thief disagreed and appealed to the Zhejiang High Court. The court, because the high court's trial period was approaching, escorted the thief to the county public security bureau yesterday for transfer. The bureau chief, Zhang Rixin, sent two police officers, Zhang Wenpin and Zhang Zaifa, to escort the thief to the Tiantai County Government. Unexpectedly, when passing through the thief's village, many bandits suddenly appeared, each holding guns and other weapons. The police were unable to resist and allowed the bandits to rob the thief away.

▲ Sending Personnel to Survey and Inspect the Lingjiang River The Lingjiang River in Linhai is being blocked by silt, which is hindering agriculture. The Zhejiang Provincial Water Conservancy Bureau has specially sent engineer Li Shanyan to Linhai to survey the river in order to plan for dredging.

Normal Schools in Jiangsu to Change Names

Nanjing, 8th The Ministry of Education issued an order on the 8th stating that the six secondary schools for boys in Jiangsu (Jiangsu, Zhenjiang, Taicang, Rugao, and Huaihai) and the two secondary schools for girls in Jiangsu and Xuzhou, having ceased recruiting ordinary senior high school students and converted to independent normal schools, should change their names to "[Place Name] Normal School." ▲ Liu Haisu's Proposal 101

▲ Improvement of the Academic Systems of Art and Music Schools

Liu Haisu has been in Beijing for several days to discuss the preparation for the Berlin Chinese Art Exhibition and the Second National Art Exhibition. He has submitted a proposal to the Ministry of Education regarding the improvement of the academic systems of art and music schools at the conference of presidents of colleges and universities convened by the Ministry of Education on the 10th of this month. An excerpt is as follows:

Our country's art and music schools are classified as category D specialized schools with a set three-year graduation period, similar to vocational schools of industry and commerce. Art and learning are the crystallization of thought and are sufficient to express national characteristics and the spirit of the times. Therefore, the goal of art and music schools in Europe and the United States is to cultivate art experts, with no fixed time limit. Their research process is similar to that of universities. From Haisu's experience, I feel that the nature of art and music schools is very different from that of other vocational specialized schools. Therefore, a three-year term is too short. It would be laughable to apply the study period of ordinary bookkeeping to students of literature and philosophy. Although our country is currently in a period of transition and does not need to seek perfection in everything, a clear distinction must be made between advanced academic learning and ordinary technology. In the field of art and music schools, whether training teachers or experts, they cannot be compared with ordinary vocational technology. In order to meet the urgent needs of society, for example, teachers of music, painting, and handicrafts can be trained quickly and regarded as similar to vocational technology, but advanced academic learning must be treated separately and cannot be mixed. In Haisu's humble opinion, the study period for art and music schools should be at least five years, and they should be changed to independent colleges. The departments attached to them for training teachers may be slightly shortened. Compared to European countries, this is already a compromise. If we consider that advanced academic learning cannot be borrowed and that students should not be superficial, then the improvement of the academic system is an urgent matter that cannot be delayed.

Hangzhou City Elementary School Work Department Achievement Exhibition 102

The Work Department includes five tasks: school affairs, family affairs, morning affairs, crafts, and business affairs. It occupies an important position in elementary school education. Since the promulgation of the Provisional Curriculum Standards, most elementary schools in various regions have been unable to implement them according to the standards due to various problems such as personnel and equipment. In view of this, the Hangzhou City Education Department planned to hold a work achievement exhibition. Over the past year, the elementary schools under the jurisdiction of Hangzhou City have paid great attention to the development of work teaching. A large-scale exhibition was held at the Provincial High School from July 5th to 10th. More than 100 schools participated, with achievements in 17 parts and more than 60 or 70 rooms. Thousands of people visited the exhibition every day. The city government specially invited experts Jiang Danshu, Ni Zhuhua, Zong Lianghuan, and Chen Wangdou to the exhibition to review the achievements. Zong and Ni also gave lectures to guide the implementation of the Work Department. After the review is completed, the city government will provide prizes to the schools with excellent achievements to encourage them. It is reported that the reviewers are generally very satisfied with the exhibits at this exhibition.

Local News

Starting in June, the Municipal Bureau of Education 103

Fully Pays Teachers and Staff of Municipal Schools

Since January 28th, Shanghai's municipal revenue has sharply decreased, resulting in a shortage of education funds. However, municipal schools, except in the war zone, have been able to maintain classes, which shows the efforts of the administrative authorities and teachers and staff. Xu Peihuang, Director of the Municipal Bureau of Education, has praised the difficult lives of teachers and staff of municipal schools and their loyalty to their duties. Yesterday, he submitted a request to Mayor Wu to fully pay salaries starting in June, taking into account the current situation of each school. The municipal government believes that the financial situation of the municipal treasury has reached its limit. The Education Bureau has previously submitted three requests to issue 70% of the salaries starting in May, but none of them have been approved. In order to consider the lives of ordinary teachers and staff, Director Xu repeatedly discussed the matter with Mayor Wu. It is reported that the mayor has agreed with great difficulty.

Another report stated that teachers and staff of the city previously went to the Municipal Bureau of Education to petition for the supplementary payment of salaries. At that time, the director was out on official business and could not meet them. On the 6th, the Education Bureau summoned the principals and teacher representatives of various schools to the bureau. The mayor's representative and the director earnestly explained the difficult situation of the city's financial difficulties and the inability to pay full salaries, and promised to find a way within the possible range. At 11:00 AM on the 7th, when teacher representatives Li Bojun and others went to the Education Bureau, Director Xu reiterated that full salaries could be paid starting in June. The issue of the municipal school teachers and staff requesting supplementary salaries has come to an end. Yesterday, the municipal school authorities convened a joint conference of principals and teacher representatives, attended by Zhao Luqing, principal of Xicheng Elementary School, Liu Yinqian, principal of Wanzhu Elementary School, Yang Jingyi, principal of Shangwen Elementary School, and the teacher representatives from these 23 schools, Qian Cijiu, Hu Huaitian, Wu Yinchun, and others, totaling 47 people. The group first elected Li Bojun, Xu Ziling, and Qian Cijiu as the presiding officers, who reported on the experience of going to the Municipal Bureau of Education to make a request. After the report was completed, the following was discussed: (1) It was resolved that no more general meetings would be convened this afternoon. (2) It was resolved to designate Li Bojun, Hu Huaitian, Xu Zihua, Zhao Luqing, Zhou Peicheng, and others as nine representatives to go to the Municipal Bureau of Education to petition and request the director to give a concrete and responsible reply regarding the full payment of salaries for May, June, and July. The representatives went to the Municipal Bureau of Education at 3:00 PM to make a request. The director personally met them and expressed acceptance of the requests made by the representatives. He solemnly declared that full salaries could be paid starting in June. The director would also do his best to report the difficult living conditions of the teachers and staff to the mayor regarding the salaries for May. (Central News Agency)

Zhang Pingjiang Founds Huiping Middle School 104

Ms. Zhang Pingjiang is the widow of the late Kuomintang veteran Huang Huiping. She participated in the so-called "Capital Revolution" in Beijing during the 14th and 15th years of the Republic. She was subsequently placed on a wanted list along with Gu (Mengyu) and Li (Shizeng). She went south to Shanghai and Hong Kong and has been working hard for the revolution ever since. She is highly regarded by many leaders of the party and the country. Recently, in view of the daily worsening of the national crisis, the increasing need for talent, and the urgent need to promote social education, and in order to mourn her deceased husband, she founded Huiping Middle School. She has already rented a large house on Avenue Joffre as a school building and will soon publish advertisements for enrollment. In addition to inviting Chen Shaobai, Wang Jingwei, Chen Gongbo, Gu Mengyu, Yu Youren, Jiang Menglin, Wu Tiecheng, Chen Shuren, Yi Peiji, Qin Zhen, Zhang Ji, and others to serve as school board members, the hired faculty and staff, such as Huang Shaoxu (Dean of Academic Affairs), Chen Lie (Director of General Affairs), Wang Zhuyi (Director of Moral Education), Sun Bojian, Wang Lixi, Jiang Zhensan, Hu Qiuyuan, Huang Xianzhang, Luo Li, Lu Jingqing, Zhang Fangzhou, Gucheng Huanghao and others, are all among the best in terms of academic ability and teaching qualifications.

Shanghai Municipal Post-War Reconstruction Education Plan (1) 108

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education yesterday drafted a "Shanghai Municipal Post-War Reconstruction Education Plan" as follows:

1. The Importance of Post-War Education Reconstruction

Since the invasion of Shanghai by the brutal Japanese army, the residences in Zhabei and other places have been reduced to ruins, and the education sector has been completely destroyed. Now that the ceasefire agreement has been signed and the national territory has been recovered, residents who fled are gradually returning to their hometowns. Although we must caress the wounds, we must also learn from the pain. As Shanghai is a world market, the focus of attention both at home and abroad, if we can actively restore various industries in a short period, we can make the friendly countries of the world understand the resilience and spirit of the Chinese nation. Moreover, the education sector, which nurtures and trains the people, cannot be delayed. Therefore, the importance of post-war education reconstruction is self-evident.

2. The Scope of Post-War Education Reconstruction

The scope of post-war education reconstruction will tentatively include Zhabei, Jiangwan, and Wusong.

3. The Timeframe for Reconstruction Completion

The timeframe for reconstruction completion is indeed an important issue. Too long would be too slow, and too short would exceed our financial capabilities. After careful consideration, it is proposed to proceed in three phases, each lasting one to one and a half years.

4. Types of Education

Post-war education reconstruction is divided into two major parts: school education and social education. They are described as follows:

(A) The School Education Reconstruction Plan is tentatively divided into three items:

(1) Number of schools to be established, (2) Location of schools to be established, and (3) School buildings and equipment. They are described as follows:

(1) Number of Schools to be Established

The Zhabei area can be divided into two parts: one is the area destroyed by the war, and the other is the area affected by the war. The destroyed area is north of the Jinghu Railway, including Qiujiang Road, Yongxing Road, Xiangshan Road, Zhongxing Road, and Zhonghua New Road, which have now become scorched earth. In this area, there were seven municipal schools, including Jiancheng, Huifeng, Peiben, Lubin, Yude, Zhabei Kindergarten, and Dexin, with a total of 31 classrooms and accommodating more than 2,000 students. There were also dozens of private elementary schools with approximately 10,000 students. This time, the school buildings of the municipal and private schools have been severely damaged. Because most of the houses in the area have been burned down, it will take some time for all the residents to return. It is proposed that in the first phase, one middle school specializing in commerce, two complete elementary schools with twelve classrooms or more and attached kindergartens, and four complete elementary schools with six grades or more and attached kindergartens will be established in the area with convenient transportation and easier recovery of the market to meet the urgent needs. The first phase can accommodate approximately 3,000 to 4,000 elementary school students to restore the number of students accommodated by the municipal elementary schools before the war. However, after the first year, as local housing construction gradually increases and residents gradually move back, the number of students will inevitably increase. Moreover, some private elementary schools will not be easy to restore. It is still necessary to plan for the gradual return of school-age children and the remedy for the loss of schooling for students in private schools. It is proposed to add four elementary schools with six classrooms or more in the second phase and one municipal middle school, one twelve-grade elementary school, and two six-grade elementary schools in the third phase to achieve universal education. As for the area affected by the war, that is, all places in the Zhabei area except the destroyed area, there were six municipal elementary schools, including Xinmin, Yongxing, Pengnan, Tanzhen, Qimei, and Haishan. These school buildings have not been severely damaged. It is proposed that in the temporary reorganization plan, five elementary schools will be reopened first, but Xinmin Elementary School will be opened at another location. Other private middle and elementary schools will also gradually recover.

Chou. Jiangwan District: The towns and villages in this area have all been damaged. The bureau had established twelve municipal elementary schools such as Qiujiang, with most of the school buildings damaged. These twelve schools have a total of thirty-seven classrooms, accommodating more than 2,000 students. In this temporary recovery plan, the partially destroyed Xijiang, Qiujiang, and the undamaged Zhongshan, Jianke, Qiandang, Luge, and Yanwan seven elementary schools will be repaired and reopened immediately. On the other hand, the parts of the Xijiang, Qiujiang, and Yanwan school buildings that were burned down will be rebuilt according to this reconstruction plan. There are also four elementary schools, Maicun, Taowan, Gaojing, and Dongjiang, and the Yujing Elementary School, which were burned down or damaged and cannot be opened at this time. It is proposed to open two elementary schools with six grades or more and attached kindergartens and four two-classroom elementary schools in the first phase to restore the number of students accommodated before the war. It is also proposed to add one municipal middle school (agricultural science), one elementary school with six classrooms or more and attached kindergartens, and three four-classroom elementary schools in the second phase. It is also proposed to expand the six-classroom elementary school established in the second phase to twelve classrooms and add one elementary school with six classrooms or more and attached kindergartens and two four-classroom elementary schools in the third phase to expand the capacity.

Yin. Wusong District: The towns and villages in this area have all been damaged. The bureau previously established eight schools, including Wusong Elementary School, and one Wusong Junior High School. The elementary schools have a total of thirty classrooms, accommodating approximately 2,000 elementary school students, and the middle school has four classrooms, accommodating more than 100 middle school students. All the schools have been damaged. In this temporary plan, the partially destroyed Wusong, Taixing, and Tancun three elementary schools will be repaired and reopened. On the other hand, the parts of the Wusong Elementary School and other school buildings that have been destroyed will be rebuilt according to the reconstruction plan. There are also five elementary schools, Peiji, Wanbei, Songbei, Chenxiang, and Haoqiao, whose school buildings have been completely or partially destroyed and cannot be opened. It is proposed to expand Wusong Junior High School into a complete middle school specializing in engineering and establish one elementary school with twelve classrooms and an attached kindergarten and four four-classroom elementary schools in the first phase. It is also proposed to establish one elementary school with six classrooms or more and attached kindergartens and two four-classroom elementary schools in the second phase. In the third phase, it is proposed to create a vocational school and add one elementary school with twelve classrooms and an attached kindergarten and two four-classroom elementary schools to achieve universal education.

Enthusiastic Farewell at the Huangpu River Wharf Yesterday Morning 109

Liu Changchun Carries the National Flag to the United States

| Attending the 10th World Games |

▲ Wang Zhengting Performs the Flag-Giving Ceremony at the Customs

▲ Boarding the Ship at 10 AM, a Large Crowd Saw Him Off

Liu Changchun, the first athlete from China to attend the World Games, and his coach, Mr. Song Junfu, boarded the President Wilson ship at 11:00 AM yesterday morning amidst enthusiastic farewells and departed Shanghai for the United States. A large crowd from all walks of life gathered at the Customs wharf to see them off, demonstrating their patriotic unity and placing infinite hope in Mr. Liu.

▲ A Solemn and Enthusiastic Flag-Giving Ceremony

The small boat carrying the passengers to the President Wilson ship left the shore at 10:00 AM. Before boarding the small boat, the flag-giving ceremony was held. At 9:30 AM, Wang Zhengting, the chairman of the China National Amateur Athletic Federation, presented Liu with a bright national flag and a triangular pennant of the federation on the Customs wharf. Liu received them respectfully. This national flag will be planted at the World Games. Wang then delivered a speech, saying that China has a long history of sports, and Mr. Liu is a famous general of our country. He hopes that he will work hard to win glory for the motherland and live up to his mission. After Liu thanked him, he boarded the small boat holding the flag. At 7:00 AM yesterday morning, the sound film production by Fox Company failed due to a broken machine.

▲ Three Cheers for the Republic of China

Wang Zhengting, accompanied by his wife and Zhao Jinqing, a director of the federation, waited at the wharf to bid farewell with great sincerity. There were also about 400 people from all walks of life who came to see them off. The small boat left the wharf at 10:00 AM sharp. Zhou Jiaqi, a staff member of the federation, led the well-wishers to shout "Long live the Republic of China" three times, the sound echoing in the sky, stirring and magnificent. As the small boat went further away, Wang and the others and those who saw him off...

▲ Farewell on the President Wilson Ship

Hao Gengsheng and friends of Song and Liu, as well as newspaper reporters, also boarded the small boat to the President Wilson ship. They arrived at the Yangshupu Pier at 10:20 AM to board the ship. The cabins of Mr. Song and Mr. Liu were number 131, which were very comfortable. The small boat returned at 10:45 AM, and the President Wilson also slowly moved. Everyone leaned on the railing and looked out, waving small towels. The figures gradually blurred until they disappeared. The well-wishers returned to Shanghai, while Mr. Song and Mr. Liu left Shanghai for Los Angeles.

The Past and Present of the World Games (4) 111

(4) The Significance of the Olympic Games

The significance of the Olympic Games is profound and broad. The words of Baron Pierre de Coubertin of France, the initiator of the modern Olympic Games, are cited to express his intentions:

(The restoration of the Olympic Games, in modern life and circumstances, brings together the peoples of the world every four years, trusting that competitions of peace and courtesy can organize the supreme form of internationalism.)

(Above all, it can preserve in athletic sports the noble and heroic qualities that made people stand out in the past, and enjoy the same admirable status in the educational position of the people of this era as the ancient Greek people's education did.)

(Competitive sports are gradually spreading all over the world and have replaced unhealthy entertainment and harmful wandering in young people's lives. People in society must have their various shortcomings. True competitive sports can eliminate their evils to promote a healthy national spirit.)

(It is still difficult to judge to what extent the Olympic concept has progressed, but judging from the various aspects of its creation, the depth of its definition is very clear: (1) create and enhance the friendly relations of peaceful communication between civilized countries; (2) clarify and eliminate the selfish and fraudulent means in competitive sports, seek games that everyone can get a fair judgment, and make the competition not a youth's joy with victory.)

In short, the World Olympic Games has three goals: social education and morality. In the social aspect, it enables people to have a spirit of mutual understanding; in the educational aspect, (1) making physical education an active and rational development (2) establishing public sports fields and sports fields; in the moral aspect, it promotes (1) the spirit that sports should have (2) the movement of the masses. In short, it is to protect and promote pure amateur sports. Dedicated and dedicated people are here.

Resolutions of the Municipal Sports Guidance Association 112

The Municipal Sports Instructors Association held a regular meeting at Yuebinlou, Daxin Street, Sanma Road at 7:00 PM the night before last. Chen Yongsheng, Du Yufei, Wang Fudan, Qian Yiqin, Li Jiyuan, Li Feiyun, Zou Yinlu, Song Zean, Gu Shunhua, Chen Yuze, and other fifteen people were present. First, the chairman Wang Fudan reported the reasons for the stagnation of the association's affairs in the past six months and the dispersal of members affected by the war. Then, it was resolved to improve the association's affairs and propose various cases to the National Sports Conference. The contents are recorded as follows: (1) Re-election of officers case. Due to the small number of attendees, it was resolved to postpone the re-election to the general meeting on September 15. Before the new officers are produced, the old officers will still be responsible. (2) Amendment of the constitution case. Because the original constitution did not have detailed regulations on membership fees, absenteeism at meetings, and questions about the loss of membership qualifications, it was resolved to appoint five people as members of the constitution amendment committee to amend this point in detail. (3) Investigation of the association's members case. It was resolved that the secretary should send letters to investigate the current situation of the association's members. (4) National Sports Conference proposal case. It was resolved that if any member of the association has a proposal for the National Sports Conference, please submit it in writing to the chairman Wang Fudan before July 20, and the chairman will be responsible for sorting it out and sending it directly to the secretariat of the National Sports Conference.

Song Ziwen Agrees with Silver and Money Industries on the 116

Principle of Abolishing Taels and Changing to Yuan

▲ It Can Be Implemented After the Government Decides

▲ From Then On, the Currency System Has Hope of Unification

Before leaving Shanghai and returning to Beijing, Minister of Finance Song Ziwen convened a meeting of leaders from the silver and money industries in this city at the Song residence on the morning of the 7th. In addition to discussing other financial issues, the issue of abolishing taels and changing to yuan was discussed in detail. The principle has been determined after consultations between Minister Song and the silver and money industries. It is only awaiting the government's decision before research can be conducted on implementation methods.

▲ According to a bank manager, the motive for changing to yuan is that the lack of unification of China's monetary system has long been a major problem for the social economy. The proposal for reform has been advocated for a long time. When Japan implemented the gold embargo and India changed to the gold standard, Minister Song Ziwen also had a motion that China should also implement the gold standard and asked the foreign advisor of the Ministry of Finance, Kailmuer, to study China's old monetary system and write a reform opinion book for implementation. However, due to Chinese customs, in addition to taels, there is also a kind of standard silver system. The reform process is complex and cannot be done urgently, so the motion was shelved. As for the motive for abolishing taels and changing to yuan this time, on the one hand, it is due to the over-complexity of the existing currency system, and on the other hand, it is due to the sharp drop in foreign cents, which is a good opportunity to change taels to yuan. Therefore, the government and merchants have this feeling and resolutely have this proposal to abolish taels and change to yuan.

▲ The Principle Has Been Determined. When Minister Song Ziwen convened a meeting of representatives of the silver and money industries the other day (the 7th) to discuss the issue of abolishing taels and changing to yuan, because the government and the business community both have the determination to reform, the discussion was very smooth. At the end of the discussion, it was completely determined. The main points are as follows: (1) Implement the abolition of silver tael calculation and completely adopt the silver yuan system to unify the currency system. (2) When completely adopting the silver yuan system, the old cast silver yuan will still be used as before. (3) Once the legal price and weight, the standard of each yuan being seven qian and one fen or seven qian and two fen is stipulated, the casting of new coins will begin. As for the silver tael system, when the implementation of the abolition, all past transactions calculated in silver taels must be discussed in detail and decided after the government decides.

▲ The silver and money industries agree. When discussing the method of abolishing taels and changing to yuan, the silver and money industries have long felt the pain of the lack of unification of the currency system. If the silver tael can be abolished and the silver yuan system can be adopted exclusively, there will be no more complicated procedures of silver tael cutting and exchange, and the intangible losses of sudden rises and falls. It will be of great benefit to financial transactions thereafter. Therefore, the four banks of China, Jiaotong, Central, Zhejiang Xingye, Zhejiang Shiye, Shanghai Bank Preparation Depot, and representatives of the money industry at that time all unanimously expressed their approval of this new opportunity to change taels to yuan and unify the currency system.

▲ Implementation is probably not far away. The principle has been determined. It is only necessary to wait for Minister Song to return to Beijing to discuss with the government again, submit it to the central official meeting for decision, and then discuss the detailed clauses and start implementation. According to the observation trend of this person (a bank manager claimed himself), now that the government and the business community both feel the convenience of unification and are determined to implement the abolition of taels and change to yuan at the extremely good opportunity of the sharp drop in foreign cents, the period of implementation should not be far away after some preparation. The estimated date is about two months, or it may be realized.

▲ Casting New Coins in Shanghai. When this method is implemented and the legal price of the new coins is determined, the Ministry of Finance must cast new coins for use. The mint in Beijing has been destroyed, and the one in Hangzhou has also stopped casting. Therefore, when casting new coins in the future, it will be cast by the Shanghai Mint. It is said that Mr. Xu Jiqing, the director of the Shanghai Mint, was retained by the Ministry of Finance when he submitted his resignation for the first time after being appointed by the central government, and the second resignation has not been approved until now. If this matter is implemented, the factory will of course have to be opened for casting, so the Ministry of Finance is still interested in Mr. Xu to take office.

▲ Foreign Exchange Relations. After the implementation of the abolition of taels and changing to yuan, there are still considerable relations in foreign exchange. Because when using taels, the exchange rate is based on the exchange rate between the British shilling and the silver tael. After changing to yuan, there is a considerable relationship between the fineness of the raw silver used for casting silver yuan and the legal price of silver yuan. Therefore, the exchange rate of silver yuan in foreign exchange should not be as high or low as when using taels.

Standards for 117

Rent Reduction in This City

▲ Announced by the Municipal Government Yesterday

▲ Rent Reduction Measures. The Municipal Council issued a proclamation yesterday, stating that since the January 28th Incident, the war has caused great damage in various places. Even the adjacent areas have not been able to live in peace. Therefore, people from all walks of life believe that if rent is not reduced appropriately, it will not be enough to provide relief. However, landlords and residents have different positions and different opinions. Disputes have arisen from holding each other. If it is delayed indefinitely, not only will the parties be at a disadvantage, but the local order and social security will be greatly affected. Renting a house is originally a contractual relationship and belongs to the judicial scope. Now, according to the submissions of both parties, there is no objection to the principle of rent exemption, but the standards for rent exemption are requested to be determined together. The mayor has considered the situation, extensively adopted public opinion, and formulated four measures and prepared illustrations, which were submitted to the Municipal Council for decision and announcement to serve as a guideline. All landlords must know that the use and benefit of leased items is a prerequisite for the payment of rent. There is a clear provision in the law, and it should be understood in particular. All residents must also know that the burden of this disaster should not be entirely placed on the industry of real estate ownership. Moreover, the situation of real estate ownership in this city is complicated. The economic capacity of the landlords may not be as the residents say. It is hoped that landlords and residents will embrace the spirit of mutual understanding and mutual assistance to achieve the goal of co-existence and co-prosperity. The future of the country, society, and the municipality depends on it. This proclamation lists the standards and methods as follows: (1) Wusong, Jiangwan, Yinhang, Zhenru, Pengpu, Yinxiang, Zhabei, and other districts (including the section of the North District that crosses the boundary and builds roads) are exempt from rent for three months. (2) The special zone north of the Suzhou River and west of Yokohama is exempt from rent for two and a half months. (3) The special zone east of Yokohama and the Yangshupu area are exempt from rent for two months. (4) The South Shanghai District and the part of the Pusong District north of the Suzhou River are exempt from rent for one month.

▲ Property Tax Exemption for One Month. The municipal government believes that the residents in the war zone have suffered huge losses. In order to sympathize with the people's difficulties, it has stipulated measures to reduce and exempt various taxes in the war zone and announced them to the public. However, the scope of implementation stipulated therein is limited to the war zone and its adjacent areas. It is now heard that the municipal government believes that although the South Shanghai District and the part of the Pusong District north of the Suzhou River have not directly suffered losses in the war, they have been indirectly affected during the war period because residents have not been able to live in peace. Now that the rent in the area has been exempted for one month after the Municipal Council's resolution, the property tax will also be reduced appropriately. At the same time, it was decided by the Municipal Council to exempt the tax for one month. It is said that it will be announced to the public soon and the Finance Bureau will be ordered to comply.

Lin Baike Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 118

▲ Detailed Conversation with Our Newspaper's Reporter

▲ Calls Sun Yat-sen the Second Christ

Mr. Lin Baike, legal advisor to the National Government, arrived in Shanghai yesterday aboard the "GeMetsinger" steamer with General Mei Renjie. He is a close friend of Mr. Sun Yat-sen, stout, balding, with many missing teeth. Dressed in white canvas clothing, he came to our office for a detailed conversation with our reporter immediately after unloading his luggage. Mr. Lin spoke frankly and had a particularly naive and endearing demeanor. What follows is the content of his conversation:

I (referring to Lin Baike himself; the same applies hereafter) was dispatched to the United States in October 1930 as a special envoy of the National Government, where I repeatedly engaged with U.S. President Hoover and leaders of the Senate and the House of Representatives to discuss the progress of silver loans. If China had not experienced further civil wars, the silver loan of 27 million taels would have been secured long ago. I had suggested two types of loans to the National Government: a silver loan and a wheat loan. The silver loan was designated for the construction of national roads, while the wheat loan was for disaster relief. American politicians are divided into two factions: one advocates exporting silver due to America's surplus silver reserves, and the other advocates exporting wheat due to America's overabundance of wheat. I took advantage of this opportunity to navigate between these two factions, and as a result, the wheat loan was successfully obtained, amounting to approximately 30 million dan of American wheat. If China had not had internal strife, the silver loan would also have been successful. In 1931, I traveled to Europe, visiting 31 locations to promote China. I firmly believe that if the Chinese government and people can unite sincerely, then the violent Japanese will be nothing to fear. If China can truly achieve unification, then there is still hope for the future, and the silver loan will not be a problem. In April of this year, while in Madrid, Spain, I received an urgent telegram from the National Government summoning me back. Therefore, I had to temporarily end my promotional work and return home with haste. After arriving in Shanghai today, I learned that my old friend Mr. Zhan Tang is in Hong Kong, and Mr. Zhesheng has also left. However, Mr. Jingwei is in Nanjing. I plan to stay in Shanghai for a short time, both to await instructions from the government and to expedite the creation of a work report. It is easier to obtain information and collect statistical materials in Shanghai for the report. Alas, I am old. I have followed Mr. Sun for 25 years. Whenever there were difficulties, Mr. Sun would resolve them with a few words. I firmly believe that if Mr. Sun were still alive, my work would proceed more smoothly. Now, however, the party lacks a leader, and the organization is disorganized. Although I am filled with enthusiasm, there is nothing I can do. I hope the people will offer well-intentioned criticism and supervision to the government, and that the government and the people will cooperate sincerely, so that there will be hope for China's future.

Lin Baike (Photo by Li Zunyong)

In his conversation with the reporter, Lin Baike repeatedly referred to Sun Yat-sen as his second Christ and presented the reporter with a copy of his recent book, "Gospel of Sun Chung Shan" ("The Mission of Sun Yat-sen"). This is noted here to express our gratitude.

Silk Factory Labor Strike 119

Resolved Yesterday Through Mediation

▲ Work Resumes for All Tomorrow

Following the labor strike at silk factories in the city, party and government authorities formally mediated yesterday, and a mediation record has been signed. Workers will resume work across the board tomorrow.

▲ Mediation Conference: Yesterday afternoon at 2 PM, the Bureau of Social Affairs convened the Labor-Management Mediation Committee to formally mediate the silk factory strike. Present were employer representatives Zhu Jing'an and Zhang Peichuo, labor representatives Zhu Xizhang and Yang Gengdi, Wang Guoxian of the Public Security Bureau, Zhou Lianze of the Municipal Party Headquarters, and Wang Xianqing of the Bureau of Social Affairs. The meeting was chaired by Wang Xianqing, with Wang Rangyu recording. The chairman first reported, and the employer representatives stated that the silk factories operating were completely acting on behalf of the silver and money trades, and that in reality, the factories and workers were in the same position. At the time, the silver and money trades had contract stipulations, setting the price at one tael and one mace and a half per cart for a period of three months. If the workers were to demand an increase in wages, the contracts would inevitably be terminated. The labor representatives stated that since the wage reduction, the workers' daily income was insufficient to cover expenses, and they requested that the factories consider an increase in order to resolve the situation as soon as possible, which would be fortunate for both labor and management. The chairman stated that he understood the workers' hardships and that he was also aware of the factory's difficulties. However, no matter how difficult the factory was, they were asked to take responsibility for a slight increase so that work could resume as soon as possible. It was not until 8 PM that labor and management reached an agreement and signed the mediation record.

▲ Original Text of the Record: Labor-Management Mediation Committee of Shanghai Municipality, Mediation Record. Disputing Parties: Labor: Industrial Union of Silk Reeling Industry, Districts 3, 4, and 6 of Shanghai Municipality, represented by Zhu Xizhang and Yang Gengdi; Management: Shanghai Silk Factory Trade Association, represented by Zhu Jing'an and Zhang Peisi. Regarding the wage dispute of the disputing parties listed on the right, the committee convened mediation, and the agreement signed by both parties is recorded as follows: 1. Due to the decline of the silk industry, employers have suffered greatly. Paying the original wages is difficult. In the spirit of labor-management cooperation, the top-grade female workers' wages will be temporarily reduced to 45 cents per person per day. The wages of other workers will be determined proportionally. 2. The female workers' applications for work and holiday bonuses will be temporarily suspended. 3. Working hours will remain the same and will not be extended. 4. Employees' salaries will be calculated monthly according to the original terms and conditions. 5. Silkworm cocoon applications will remain as they are. 6. Employers agree to resume work on the 10th of this month, and workers must return to work as usual. 7. These conditions will be effective from the date of signing until December of this year. This agreement has been reached with the consent and signatures of both parties and should be regarded as a labor agreement between the disputing parties. Chairman: Wang Xianqing; Committee Members: Yang Gengdi, Zhu Xizhang, Zhu Jing'an, Zhang Peisi, Zhou Lianze, Wang Guoxian; Observers: Tang Binggan, Fei Danru, Wu Suzhen, Liu Sanbao, 娻巧珍, Yan Aizhu, Yang Shumei, Xia Linzhi, Cui Abao, Yuan Yunlong, Le Xiaorong, Gu Xiaomei, Chen Laohai, Chen Jilin. July 8th, 21st Year of the Republic of China.

I asked from where this expenditure was calculated. Currently, the contract prices of each factory are between one tael and five mace to one tael and one qian. According to the wage of four jiao and two fen, this is not enough to cover expenses. This is because these old cocoons were mortgaged to the silver and money trades by the factory. Now, without the funds to redeem them, we must代成絲 [unable to ascertain meaning], wait for the opportunity to sell them, and fulfill our obligations. Today, after reading the newspaper, the financial community has questioned the factory, accusing it of wanting to profit during this extremely serious period, and expressing great indignation. May I ask if the labor union will take responsibility for this inaccurate report?" The labor union representative denied making this statement and promised to send a letter to each newspaper to correct it. (Note: this newspaper did not publish this statement). Then, the Bureau of Social Affairs mediated. The chairman, Wang Bing, sincerely mediated between labor and management, repeatedly advising each representative, and it was not until 5:30 PM that an agreement was reached. The mediation resulted in a total of six articles. (1) (the above is omitted)." Chairman Zhu stated, "This labor strike coincided with Chairman Shen's trip to Hangzhou. With the entrustment of our colleagues, although the matter has been resolved, I feel deeply indebted during this time of great difficulty for our colleagues, as we still want to increase the burden. I hope everyone will understand." At this point, a representative from a certain factory stood up and said, "This labor strike was handled by Chairman Zhu and the seven representatives including Mr. Zhang Peisi, who traveled back and forth and held meetings with the labor union representatives for days. They were exceptionally tired. Now that the matter has been resolved, our colleagues should express our gratitude." At this point, all the representatives stood up to express their gratitude, and then the bell was rung to adjourn the meeting. It was already 7:30 PM.

▲ Municipal Government Instruction: The Municipal Government yesterday issued an instruction to the Public Security Bureau and the Bureau of Social Affairs regarding the silk factory strike in the city, stating, "For the purpose of ordering, this office has investigated the case of the silk factory strike in the city. The Silk Factory Trade Association's committee had previously submitted a request for protection to the government, and the government ordered the bureau to work with the Bureau of Social Affairs to handle the matter diligently. Now, according to a confidential report, the relationship between labor and management in the industry was originally harmonious. The disputes were instigated by unscrupulous individuals, and the workers who understood the situation have been automatically returning to work for days but have been prevented from gathering and threatened. They are determined to destroy what little is left of our country's silk industry." Based on this, the production of silk is one of our country's major industries. In recent years, sales have stagnated, and it is declining daily. Both labor and management in the industry should sincerely cooperate and work together to save it. Even members of society agree that the only silk industry left in our country cannot withstand further destruction. However, these unscrupulous elements have other motives, instigating strikes and engaging in destruction, which is deplorable. In addition to ordering the Bureau of Social Affairs to quickly investigate the facts of the labor-management dispute and handle it impartially, this office urgently orders the bureau to comply and immediately and closely investigate and arrest the individuals instigating the labor strike, protect the workers' return to work, and report the handling situation without delay. This order. (The text of the order to the Bureau of Social Affairs is omitted.)

Party and Government Authorities Mediate Yesterday 120

Labor Strike at French Water and Electricity Company

▲ No Results

Following the strike by all staff and workers of the Mechanical Affairs Department of the French Water and Electricity Company, party and government authorities attempted mediation yesterday but were unable to find a solution. The municipal government sent a special envoy to consult with the French consul, and all workers held a general meeting, further escalating the situation. The company is protected by French soldiers. Details are as follows:

▲ Strike Situation Yesterday: Staff and workers in all departments of the Mechanical Affairs Department continued their strike yesterday and reported to the Strike Committee. They gathered at the Water and Electricity Industry Union in the Second District of the Dada Lane on Luban Road. The Second District Police Station of the Municipal Public Security Bureau was ordered to dispatch police to maintain order. All pickets wore symbols and patrolled. The iron gates of the company at the Luban Road entrance were tightly closed, and Chinese and foreign detectives were stationed around to protect the company. Staff and workers in the Vehicle Affairs Department continued to work as usual, so streetcars and buses on various routes of the French company continued to operate as usual.

▲ Party and Government Officials Sent to Mediate: Zhu Guilin of the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, Zhong Quan of the Municipal Party Headquarters, and Zhou Lianze were ordered to meet at 11:15 AM yesterday with Zhang Fubao, director of the Second District Water and Electricity Industry Union, and Shen Jingyi, the workers' representative, to attempt mediation at the company. The comprador Xu Jingshan notified the manager Gu Qiya, who refused to meet with the union and worker representatives. After strenuous efforts proved ineffective, the party and government officials met with the manager and explained the reason for their mediation. The manager stated that the company was a French company located in the French concession, and that the workers' demands had been submitted to the French consul and board of directors for handling, so a response could not be given at this time. However, point four, the subsidy fee, had already been approved to be paid to the workers. If the workers were willing to resume work unconditionally, they could go directly to work, and he hoped they would be persuaded to resume work. The party and government officials repeatedly explained to no avail, and they withdrew at 12:20 PM.

▲ Warning to Working Staff: After the staff and workers of the Mechanical Affairs Department went on strike, the office, ordering department, and comprador department, totaling 45 staff members, continued to work as usual yesterday. The Strike Committee issued a special warning yesterday, stating, "Since the strike, the majority of workers and staff have come to the committee. However, a small number of staff members have tried to ingratiate themselves with the 方 [unclear] and undermine the labor movement, continuing to work as usual. The general meeting has resolved to warn these staff members to leave the factory and come to the committee immediately, or they will be dealt with according to the method for dealing with running dogs. This is hereby announced for your information."

▲ General Meeting in the Afternoon: At 3 PM yesterday, the Second District Water and Electricity Industry Union held a general meeting of all members at the intersection of Luban Road and Dada Lane. Zhong Quan of the Municipal Party Headquarters and Zhu Guilin of the Bureau of Social Affairs attended to provide guidance. The Municipal Public Security Bureau dispatched armed police to provide protection. More than 800 members attended. Shen Jingyi was publicly elected as chairman and reported on the strike. Then, discussions began. (1) The case of Xu Amei, the former executive director of the union, was resolved as follows: A. Request the company to prove that Xu Amei is not a communist. B. Have all the workers send a letter to the court to prove it. C. Wages will be paid during his time in prison. D. Reinstate his job after his release. E. 求訓 [Seek training] from the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Bureau of Social Affairs to provide assistance. F. Issue a declaration that he was falsely imprisoned. (2) The case of Zhu Along and 21 others in the wiring department was resolved as follows: A. Demand immediate reinstatement. B. Wages will be paid for the period of the work stoppage. (3) The case of Shao Ziying, who was dismissed by the company without cause, was resolved as follows: Reinstate his position. (4) The question of whether the union's operating funds should be increased was resolved as follows: Increase to 500 yuan per month. (5) The question of paying wages during the strike was resolved as follows: Pay both long-term and short-term workers. (6) The case of Lu Guan Hong was resolved as follows: Send a letter to the company to dismiss him and investigate. (7) The question of increasing rent subsidies was resolved as follows: Six yuan per person per month. (8) The question of increasing the wages of both skilled and unskilled workers by 15% was resolved as follows: Passed. (9) The question of issuing uniforms to all employees was resolved as follows: Passed. (10) Existing labor-management conditions will remain in effect. (11) Those who violate strike discipline, such as employees who continue to work as usual, will be dismissed. (12) Those who work every month without taking leave will be eligible to apply for four工 [unclear]. The meeting adjourned at 5 PM.

▲ Municipal Government Conducting Consultations: The manager of the French Water and Electricity Company claimed that the workers' demands had been submitted to the French consul and board of directors for handling, which caused obstacles to the mediation efforts of the party and government officials yesterday. It is reported that the Municipal Government, in order to resolve the French electricity strike as soon as possible, will send officials to consult with the French consul to find a solution and avoid the expansion of the labor strike.

▲ French Soldiers Protect the Company: According to sources at the company, the case of Shao Ziying is not considered a dismissal but a termination. The reason is that the position of meter reading supervisor is no longer needed. However, the workers believe that the company's business has been booming for years, so there is no reason to eliminate the position. Also, after the general meeting of all workers yesterday, the company suddenly increased the number of armed French Annamite soldiers by four teams, about 100 men, led by French officers, who entered the company in the evening to guard and protect it.

Electrical Machinery and Silk Weaving Trade Association 122

Thoroughly Investigate Inferior Silk

▲ Aimed at Promoting Domestic Products

The Shanghai Electrical Machinery and Silk Weaving Factory Trade Association recently heard rumors among its members that they were purchasing inferior silk cocoons. This not only concerns the reputation of all silk weaving factories but will also destroy the fate of domestic goods. Therefore, it convened a special emergency meeting yesterday. Many well-known silk weaving manufacturers in Shanghai attended. The important resolutions are as follows: (1) Send a letter to the Jianghai Customs to investigate whether Japanese silk cocoons have been imported in recent months. (2) Dispatch investigating committee members Wang Shiqiang, Wang Baotai, Tong Xinbo, and Qian Boxi to secretly visit various factories to thoroughly investigate the raw materials of the textiles. (3) Publish announcements in the Shen, Xin, and Min newspapers, offering a reward. If anyone finds that members of the trade association are privately purchasing inferior silk cocoons and obtains evidence, they will be sent to this association and will be rewarded with 500 yuan. The rest is omitted. The letter to the Jianghai Customs states, "We are writing to you to say that promoting domestic products is the inherent responsibility of citizens. Silk is the earliest invention in our country and has a long history. It occupies an important position among export goods. However, in recent years, without knowing how to study it, it has plummeted. Thinking of this, we are deeply saddened. This association is a silk weaving organization in Shanghai, and we should do our utmost to promote domestic silk in order to reverse the loss of rights and interests and avoid being ridiculed by foreigners. Recently, we heard that a large batch of Japanese silk cocoons has been imported into this city, causing unscrupulous merchants to act against their conscience and secretly use them. The impact is huge, hindering both the national economy and people's livelihoods. We do not know if this rumor is based on facts. This office is the general hub of taxation, and we must be able to clearly indicate whether Japanese silk cocoons have come to Shanghai. Can you please provide detailed information on whether there have been any imports each month since March of this year until today, and copy down the monthly import quantities one by one? This concerns the public interest, and we hope for your sympathy. We are sending this letter accordingly and ask you to investigate. The reward announcement says, "Recently, there have been rumors outside that some people in the silk weaving industry are purchasing inferior silk cocoons, and the newspapers have even printed it, which seems to be accurate. This is deeply disturbing. Do members of this association's silk weaving factories actually purchase and use inferior silk cocoons? This has a great impact on the reputation of our colleagues. If we do not investigate immediately, it will be difficult to distinguish right from wrong. In addition to secretly dispatching special personnel to conduct a thorough investigation, this association is offering a reward of 500 yuan. If anyone finds that members of the trade association are privately purchasing inferior silk cocoons and obtains solid evidence that can be used as proof, they will be sent to this association and will be given the reward of 500 yuan. The funds have been deposited and await fulfillment. We will not go back on our word. Otherwise, malicious people will spread rumors, not only damaging the reputation of our industry but also destroying the fate of domestic goods. This concerns the development of industry and commerce, and is obviously malicious. Once this association has verified it, we will strictly investigate these rumor-mongers according to law to deter others from following suit. This is hereby announced."

Investigating Group's Attitude Towards 123

Chinese and Japanese Written Statements

According to a certain important Chinese representative who recently returned from the North, the representative office submitted more than 20 written statements to the investigating group, explaining in detail the events of the September 18th Incident and the brutality of the Japanese army. They also exposed the Japanese policy of aggression against us over the past decades, as well as all kinds of actions that violated international law and international treaties and violated or exceeded the Sino-Japanese treaties. In addition, the background of the 21 Demands and parallel lines issues was also explained in detail. Regarding the 21 Demands, particular attention was paid to the forced signing and the points denied by the parliament, explaining our country's position. Regarding the parallel lines issue, during the Sino-Chinese representatives' conference on the Eastern Three Provinces Treaty in the 31st year of Guangxu, it was not recorded in the treaty, and it must not be regarded as an obligation under the treaty. These and other reasons were repeatedly stated. At the same time, the Japanese side also submitted various written statements, attacking our country with all their might. In particular, they arbitrarily accused us of violating treaties and failing to fulfill treaty obligations. After receiving the written statements from both sides, the investigation group stated that they were still studying them and did not express any opinions. However, it is reported that they were quite dissatisfied with the Japanese side's various acts of aggression that disregarded public law and treaties, and advocated that the dignity of the treaty must be maintained. However, they also found it strange that our country denied the 21 Demands treaty. Furthermore, the Japanese side used Manchukuo as a puppet and actively proceeded with the annexation of the Northeast, disregarding all public and international laws. All past cases in the Eastern Provinces and all vested rights were entrusted to the puppet state, which was deemed to have been resolved. There was no need to negotiate with our side based on the Sino-Japanese treaty. Therefore, the Japanese felt that there was no need to study the legal effect of the 21 Demands treaty. The Japanese side's attitude was so tough that the investigation group found it very difficult, etc.

There is also Talk of Direct Sino-Japanese Negotiations 124

The Continental News reports that, according to reliable sources in this port, the National Government has decided to hold direct Sino-Japanese negotiations to resolve the Manchurian issue. However, these negotiations will be held in a country会议 [meeting] , and all countries related to the Far East will be invited to participate. It is claimed that the discussions at the meeting must be based on the Nine-Power Treaty of the Washington Conference. However, there is now an indication that China may agree to the five basic principles proposed by Japan at the League of Nations General Assembly last October. These five basic principles are those that the Japanese claim must be used as the basis for the Manchurian negotiations: (1) China and Japan mutually guarantee not to intensify the situation and to protect each other's territorial integrity. (2) All anti-Japanese activities in China, including boycotting Japanese goods, should be permanently stopped. (3) Give guarantees for the safety of life and property of Japanese residents in China. (4) Railways built in Manchuria will be paid for with Japanese funds, and existing agreements on railway construction in Manchuria will be recognized. (5) Recognize existing treaty rights, including Japanese residents' commercial lease rights in Manchuria. It is reported that the National Government has decided to hold direct negotiations because domestic scholars have been commenting on its improper reliance on the League of Nations. All the basic principles guiding the direct negotiations have been agreed upon after being proposed by Executive Yuan President Wang Jingwei and Military Affairs Commission Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. It is also said that the overall plan for direct negotiations was drafted by Wang Jingwei and then submitted for discussion at the Lushan Conference.

The French Concession Police Have Prosecuted the Russian Beggar Case 130

▲ The Special Court No. 2 Held a Hearing Yesterday Afternoon

In the case of the death of Russian beggar Georgie Ladigaiff due to illness, the French Concession Police Department, based on the report of Simon Glandigoff, who claimed to be the deceased's brother, believed that the courthouse detention center was indeed negligent and committed an act of injury causing death. Therefore, they have been conducting investigations in recent days, sparing no effort. It was originally scheduled to formally prosecute the case to the court a few days ago and, knowing that they had no right to review, they voluntarily abandoned the request for review. However, the police officially filed the lawsuit with the court only on the afternoon of the day before yesterday. After receiving the complaint, the court immediately conducted a public hearing by Judge Wang Gangxu of the Second Criminal Court at 2:00 PM yesterday. The President of the Special Court No. 2, Ying Shi, also personally went to the court to listen to the hearing, considering the importance of the case. The details of each situation are recorded as follows:

▲ Reasons for the Police Prosecution: The case was scheduled to be heard yesterday morning, but due to the congestion of cases in the morning, it was changed to 2:30 PM yesterday. The police are prosecuting a total of three people: (1) Xu Chongwen, the warden of the detention center, (2) Yu Minggao, the forensic doctor, and (3) Zhou Zongxiang, the guard of the detention center. The warden of the detention center, Xu Chongwen, and the forensic doctor, Yu Minggao, are being prosecuted for negligence under the second paragraph of Article 310 of the Criminal Code. Another defendant, Zhou Zongxiang, the guard of the detention center, is being prosecuted for injury under Article 295 of the Criminal Code. During the court hearing, the police lawyer, Fei Xizhen, stood up and stated the reasons for the prosecution, requesting that this case involve a person who was arrested by the police on June 16, sent to the court on the 17th, and died on the 19th. His name was Georgie Ladigaiff, also known as Georgie Glandigoff. Now, his brother, Simon Glandigoff, reported to the police administrative agency that his brother was beaten to death by the guard in the detention center. After receiving the report, the police immediately began to investigate and prosecuted the three defendants based on the above conditions. However, the police have not yet notified the plaintiff and witnesses in this case because they did not know in advance that the court had scheduled a trial.

▲ Warden's Testimony: After the police lawyer finished his statement, Judge Wang began to ask the first defendant, Xu Chongwen, the warden of the detention center, about his age and origin, and his reasons for defense. After Xu stated his age and origin, he said that he had three reasons to declare to the court: (1) According to the police delivery form and the court's deposit slip, it was noted that the deceased Russian criminal was named Georgie Ladigaiff. Now, the police suddenly has another name, Georgie Glandigoff. The judge should determine whether the above two names refer to the same person. (2) The delivery form at the time stated that the criminal had no home, no occupation, and no residence. Now, someone claiming to be his brother has come forward to sue. Whether this person is the deceased's brother. (3) The police accused the cause of death as being beaten to death and also as being negligent. In law, the two crimes cannot be prosecuted at the same time. Therefore, it should be determined how the deceased died. The deceased was already ill before entering the detention center. When he was sent to the court for trial, he could not stand in court. This was witnessed by the judge and the police lawyer at the time. When he was sent to the detention center at 4:00 PM on June 17, I immediately asked forensic doctor Yu for a diagnosis because he was ill. Forensic doctor Yu arrived at the detention center at about 5:00 PM, and after the diagnosis, he gave him a relieving drink. The next morning, the condition improved slightly. Forensic doctor Yu came to the detention center again at 9:00 AM and 5:00 PM for diagnosis and treatment. Because the condition had improved slightly, he did not advocate sending him to the hospital. According to Article 50 of the prison regulations, the person in charge of the prison is not required to send sick prisoners to the hospital. Moreover, the patient had received a diagnosis from a forensic doctor and had improved slightly, so he did not advocate transferring him to the hospital at that time. Unexpectedly, on the morning of the 19th, according to the guard's report, the patient's condition suddenly became serious. I immediately ordered someone to ask forensic doctor Yu for diagnosis again. At that time, forensic doctor Yu believed that the patient had cholera, and the condition was very serious and should be sent to the hospital. He then ordered the guard to prepare the transfer procedures. Unexpectedly, before the procedures were completed, the patient died at 11:40 AM. The deceased died of cholera. There are many symptoms of cholera, some infectious and some non-infectious. The deceased was said to have non-infectious cholera, so the three Russian criminals in the same prison at the same time were not infected. This is the process of the deceased's admission to the hospital and death.

▲ Testimony of Forensic Doctor Yu: After the first defendant, Xu Chongwen, the warden of the detention center, finished his testimony, the court immediately interrogated the second defendant, forensic doctor Yu Minggao. Yu testified that he was a Chinese medicine practitioner. The deceased Russian criminal was imprisoned in the detention center on June 17 after being sentenced. Because he was ill, he went to the detention center at about 5:00 PM that afternoon for diagnosis and treatment. He found that the patient was suffering from heatstroke and gave him a relieving drink. He went to the detention center for a follow-up examination the next morning. Because the patient was sleeping soundly, the jailer reported that the condition had improved slightly. He gave the jailer some "ping'an san" powder and ordered him to give it to the patient when he woke up. He went to the detention center for diagnosis and treatment again in the afternoon, but the condition did not change. Unexpectedly, at about 10:00 AM on the 19th, someone suddenly reported that the condition had suddenly changed. It happened to be raining that day, but when he went to the detention center for diagnosis and treatment as usual, he found that the patient was vomiting, diarrhea, and sweating. According to (omitted), those with vomiting, diarrhea, and excessive sweating were very dangerous and could not be saved. He ordered him to be sent to the hospital for treatment, but he heard that he died before he could be sent to the hospital. After the testimony was completed, the court asked whether the clinic only had "ping'an san" powder and "relieving water" as medicines, or whether there were other methods of treatment besides these two medicines. Yu (forensic doctor) said that the treatment in the clinic was all determined by the diagnosis and medicine was given according to the illness, and there were no regulations.

▲ Testimony of Guard Zhou: After forensic doctor Yu finished his testimony, the court immediately summoned the third defendant, guard Zhou Zongxiang. According to Zhou, he has been a guard for nine months and is in charge of prison cells No. 1 to No. 7. No. 4 is where the deceased Georgie Ladigaiff was detained. Before that, the prison only held one Russian. On June 17, at about 4:00 PM, three more Russians were detained. Before the three Russians entered the prison, one of them could not walk and was supported by two Russians. Later, the one who could not walk was Georgie Ladigaiff. Because he was ill at the time, he was placed in a ward. After the ward was arranged, forensic doctor Yu was invited to the prison for treatment. After the forensic doctor Yu diagnosed and treated him, he ordered him to drink the relieving water. The patient did not have dinner that night. On the 18th, the condition improved slightly. He had a small amount of breakfast. Forensic doctor Yu came to the prison for diagnosis and treatment once in the morning and once in the afternoon and gave him happy water powder to drink. On the morning of the 19th, the condition suddenly changed. He was vomiting and diarrhea, and the condition was very serious. He urgently reported to Warden Xu and asked forensic doctor Yu to diagnose and treat him again. Forensic doctor Yu said that the condition was extremely dangerous and ordered him to be sent to the hospital. Unexpectedly, before he could be sent to the hospital, he died at 11:40 AM. This is the fact of the deceased's passing. I did not have any beating incidents at first. After Zhou's testimony, the court asked whether the deceased had any injuries on his body when he was detained. Zhou testified that the deceased's (omitted) did not have any injuries, but he did not examine his body and did not know. The court ordered Zhou to provide a guarantor.

▲ Reschedule Trial: After Zhou Zongxiang finished his testimony, it was already 4:00 PM. At this time, Pu Laimai, the lawyer representing the plaintiff, Simon Glandigoff, had rushed to the court at 3:15 PM after hearing the news and was sitting silently in a corner. He was very calm. However, before the adjournment, the police lawyer, Fei Xizhen, stood up again and stated that the reason for the police prosecution was that the charges of injury and negligence were brought at the same time because the corpse had not yet been re-examined and it was impossible to determine. Therefore, the cause of death or the disease that caused the death should be examined during the re-examination. At that time, the police lawyer submitted the (omitted) of the deceased (omitted). The court ordered that the hearing be rescheduled to 9:00 AM on July 11 and ordered the plaintiff and witnesses to be summoned to court for questioning next time. The date of the re-examination has not yet been determined.

▲ Re-examination Next Monday: The court now believes that since the case has been formally prosecuted by the police, the judge in charge will schedule a re-examination. The date of the re-examination has not yet been determined. However, the court hopes to move the corpse of the deceased to Shanghai for re-examination next Monday morning so that the truth of the case can be revealed as soon as possible. The forensic doctor for the re-examination should have been arranged by the prosecutor's office of the Special Court. Now, in order to avoid suspicion, the Special Court No. 2 has decided to hire another well-known forensic doctor to take charge or have the prosecutor's office of the High Court No. 3 send someone to inspect it to ensure impartiality.
