Shanghai Second Special District Local Court 207

▲Criminal Judgement: Qian Gengkang guilty of selling opium, sentenced to six months imprisonment and fined 1,000 yuan; 37 boxes of prepared opium (weighing 18.5 pounds), 2 liang of raw opium, 3 weighing scales, 1 knife, 4 scissors, 1 opium pipe, and 1 ledger confiscated.▲Li Yongfu guilty as a repeat offender of providing premises for opium smoking for profit, sentenced to eight months imprisonment and fined 80 yuan; Chen Shuanglin and Shen Ding'shi each guilty of one count of opium smoking, sentenced to one month imprisonment and fined 20 yuan each; Chen Shuanglin and Shen Ding'shi given a two-year suspended sentence; smoking paraphernalia, etc., confiscated as listed.▲Mao Yong'sheng guilty of providing premises for opium smoking for profit, sentenced to six months imprisonment and fined 50 yuan; Gu Zhuping guilty of one count of opium smoking, sentenced to one month imprisonment and fined 20 yuan; Gu Zhuping given a two-year suspended sentence; smoking paraphernalia, etc., confiscated as listed.▲Fang Yueqing guilty of providing premises for smoking opium substitutes for profit, sentenced to six months imprisonment and fined 80 yuan; Zhang Baoqing guilty of one count of smoking opium substitutes, sentenced to two months imprisonment and fined 20 yuan; Zhang Baisheng, Yu Atang, and Yu Li'shi each guilty of one count of smoking opium substitutes, sentenced to one month imprisonment and fined 10 yuan each; Zhang Baisheng and Yu Li'shi both given a two-year suspended sentence; smoking paraphernalia, red pills, etc., confiscated as listed.▲Qin Wangshi and Yang Xiaoqin each guilty of one count of opium smoking, sentenced to one month imprisonment and fined 20 yuan each; Qin Wangshi and Yang Xiaoqin both given a two-year suspended sentence; smoking paraphernalia, etc., confiscated as listed.▲Plaintiff Yang Daoqing sues Xia Ziyang for negligent injury and false accusation; Xia Chaiyang guilty of professional negligence causing injury, fined 200 yuan; Yang Daoqing not guilty.▲Police Department sues Ai Bairaalici Shanshier et al. for morphine related offenses; Ai Bairaalici Shanshier and Ai Bairaalici Jia Tuolina both not guilty.▲Zhu Ada, repeat offender for theft, sentenced to five months imprisonment.▲Lu Yonghe, repeat offender for theft, sentenced to six months imprisonment; Zhang Guiyi guilty of smoking opium substitutes, sentenced to six months imprisonment; Yao Bingsheng, repeat offender for smoking opium substitutes, sentenced to two months imprisonment; Zhang A'er, Shi Gen, Qian Gu, Yin Hu, Lu Zhang'shi, and Zhang Wenkuai each sentenced to one month imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes.▲Jin Genrong sentenced to six months imprisonment for providing premises for smoking opium substitutes; Shen Guisheng and Shen Tiejun, repeat offenders for smoking opium substitutes, each sentenced to two months imprisonment; Chen Xinggen, Pan Zhiqin, He Xiqin, and Song Jiaxiang each sentenced to one month imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes; Pan Zhiqin and He Xiqin both given a two-year suspended sentence.▲He Shu'shi sentenced to six months imprisonment for providing premises for smoking opium substitutes; Wang Liansheng sentenced to two months imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes; Fu Gengsheng, repeat offender for smoking opium substitutes, sentenced to three months imprisonment; Wang Liansheng given a two-year suspended sentence.▲Wang Rongkang sentenced to six months imprisonment for providing premises for opium smoking; Xu Rongshan and Chen Bingsheng each sentenced to one month imprisonment for opium smoking; Xu Rongshan given a two-year suspended sentence.▲Wu Zhengquan, repeat offender for administering morphine injections for profit, sentenced to one year imprisonment; Zhu Jianru, repeat offender for receiving morphine injections, sentenced to three months imprisonment.▲Wang Xianming and Chen Axing each sentenced to two months imprisonment for opium smoking.▲Wang Deming guilty of selling opium, sentenced to one year imprisonment and fined 2,000 yuan; 51 pounds of raw opium, 1 scale, 1 pipe, 1 pair of scissors, and 1 leather sheet all confiscated and destroyed; Ge Zilong, Zhang Mingyou, Mao Wenming, Li Ziwen, Chen Ziying, and Jia Wuming all not guilty.▲Yang Arong fined 50 yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia.▲Chen Wangshi fined 30 yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia.▲He Binggui and Shang Jinsheng each sentenced to two months imprisonment for opium smoking; Shang Jinsheng given a two-year suspended sentence.▲Jiang Jintao sentenced to six months imprisonment for providing premises for opium smoking; Zhu Ashun sentenced to one month imprisonment for opium smoking; Zhu Ashun given a two-year suspended sentence.▲Wu Rongquan sentenced to six months imprisonment for providing premises for smoking opium substitutes for profit; Wang Changgen, Shen Wenkui, Wang Jinsheng, Zhang Yonglin, and Liu Aquan each sentenced to one month imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes; Wang Changgen and Shen Wenkui both given a two-year suspended sentence.

▲Criminal Instructions: Ding Hongfei and Zhang Yongfa petition for the parole of Li Chenshi; upon reviewing the petition, the matter of parole should be submitted to the head of the relevant prison for review; you are hereby notified.

Shanghai Local Court 208

▲Civil Judgement: Shi Zhaoyin versus Xie He'yin for arrears; the plaintiff's claim is dismissed; the plaintiff shall bear the litigation costs proportionally.▲Shen Mingwen versus Chen Yuqi et al. for execution objection; the plaintiff's claim is dismissed; the plaintiff shall bear the litigation costs.▲Ling Yisheng versus Wu Luping et al. for execution objection; the plaintiff's claim is dismissed; the plaintiff shall bear the litigation costs.▲Wang Zengshi versus Song Zhanglang for loan arrears; the defendant shall repay the plaintiff 250 yuan; the defendant shall bear the litigation costs.▲Zhao Xunru versus Peng Juzhou for loan arrears; the defendant shall repay the plaintiff 400 yuan, with monthly interest at a rate of 1.3% per month from the first day of the current year to the end of the execution; the remainder of the plaintiff's claim is dismissed; the plaintiff shall bear one-third of the litigation costs related to the dismissed portion, and the defendant shall bear two-thirds of the litigation costs.▲Sake versus Bi Jincai for rent arrears; the defendant shall pay the plaintiff 360 yuan in rent; the defendant shall bear the litigation costs.

▲Criminal Judgement: Hong A'gen embezzlement case; Hong A'gen sentenced to twenty days of detention for embezzling another's property.▲Chen Hesong et al. marriage interference case; Ye Peng'shi sentenced to three months imprisonment for adultery; Chen Hesong sentenced to two months imprisonment for having sexual relations with her.▲Zhang Tianlong family interference case; Zhang Tianlong sentenced to eight months imprisonment for attempting to seduce and entice a woman under the age of twenty away from the person with parental rights.▲Xing Maoyu family interference case; Xing Maoyu sentenced to one year and six months imprisonment for enticing for profit a woman under the age of twenty away from the person with parental rights.▲Xu A'gen et al. robbery case; Xu A'gen sentenced to life imprisonment and deprived of civil rights for jointly committing robbery and injuring two or more people; Xu Xiaomao not guilty; Xu A'gen shall compensate Huang Xiaozhou 120 yuan in silver, 22 jiao in small coins, and one gold bracelet.▲Ping Laosan family interference case; Ping Laosan sentenced to seven months imprisonment for enticing a woman under the age of twenty away from the person with parental rights; Ping Laosan shall return Liu Guifeng to Liu Zilin.▲Lin Ye'shi et al. sue Shang Qingyun for opium, bigamy, and false accusation; the plaintiff's claim is dismissed.▲Wang Li'shi opium case; Wang Li'shi sentenced to three months imprisonment for possessing opium with intent to sell.▲He Dexiu assault case; He Dexiu sentenced to thirty-five days of detention for injuring another's body; He Dexiu shall compensate Zhou Shunkun 31 yuan in medical expenses.▲Jiang Quanmao stolen goods case; Jiang Quanmao sentenced to forty-five days of detention for harboring stolen goods.▲Lin Zhangshi et al. family interference case; Lin Zhangshi's sentence reduced to four months imprisonment for enticing a man under the age of twenty away from the person with parental rights; Guo Liangwan and Shen Gengsheng each sentenced to six months imprisonment for enticing a man under the age of twenty away from the person with parental rights, with a three-year suspended sentence.

▲Public Notice: Wang Xinguan versus Chuan Baoshan et al. regarding a loan arrears case; the court has scheduled a public hearing for 8:00 AM on July 28th; this is a public notice.▲Zhu Liangfu versus Qiufeng Woolen Mill regarding a goods arrears case; the court has scheduled a public hearing for 8:00 AM on July 27th; this is a public notice (Above are for July 8th)
